## §0. Scope and conventions

### §0.1 What this document is

`udt_active_results.md` consolidates the load-bearing-now state of the UDT investigation:

- Standing canonical baseline at session-current state (§1)
- α = +2 baseline as WKB-phase-averaged limit of CG §4.5b canonical transport identity (§2; S68-004 reframe)
- Active D-items registry (§3 — pending S64-003)
- Formal F-flag registry + marker convention (§4 — pending S64-004)
- Composite-matter Phase 2 forward-arc (§5 stub at active doc; full content retired to IH §49.10 at S74-005)
- Predictive scorecard + standing prohibitions (§6 — pending S64-006)

### §0.2 Relationship to other documents

| Document | Role |
|---|---|
| `udt_canonical_geometry.md` (CG) | Canonical-physics document. Theorems + derivations + equations at canonical-record. This document **cross-references** CG; **does not duplicate** content. |
| `udt_active_results.md` (this document) | Active load-bearing-now consolidation. Authoritative source for status checks, anchors, open problems, vigilance disciplines. |
| `udt_validated_results.md` (archived VR) | Historical record of session verdicts + audit landings + dispatch arc summaries + retracted framings. Source from which this document was reconstructed; ARCHIVE banner landed at S64-008 (2026-05-14). |
| `udt_investigation_history.md` (IH) | Retired scaffold-character content + negative results + cleanup-arc retirement records. |
| `CLAUDE.md` | Project rules + standing canonical results block + lineage rule counter status. |
| `manuscript/human_ai.md` §24+ | Authoritative source for **lineage rule wording**. |

### §0.3 Conventions

- Cross-references to CG use the form **CG §N.M**.
- Cross-references to archived VR use the form **archived VR §N** (explicit "archived" prefix to distinguish from active content; references survive the S64-008 archive banner).
- Cross-references to IH use the form **IH §N.M**.
- Active D-items, F-flags, and lineage rule counter status carry a session-anchor when applicable (e.g., "at S63 close").
- Per-dispatch pulled-content classification (PORT-VERBATIM / CONSOLIDATION / RESTATEMENT) is registered in the S64 dispatch deliverables (`dispatch_S64_NNN_*/`), not duplicated in this document.

### §0.4 Reconstruction provenance

This document was reconstructed from archived VR over Session 64 dispatches S64-002 through S64-008. Design protocol: `dispatch_S64_001_ponder/RECONSTRUCTION_PROTOCOL.md`.

## §1. Standing canonical baseline

The load-bearing canonical results that persist across sessions. Curated source: `CLAUDE.md` "Standing canonical results" block; canonical-content sources at CG / archived VR cited per entry.

### §1.1 UDT metric (canonical reference)

The canonical metric is DERIVED at **CG §1.0** (sympy-verified per S58-009):

$$ds^2 = -e^{-2\phi(r)}\,c^2\,dt^2 + e^{2\phi(r)}\,dr^2 + r^2\,d\Omega^2$$

with $g_{tt}\,g_{rr} = -c^2$ as derived identity (consequence of GR + positional-dilation postulate under matter consistency $T^t{}_t = T^r{}_r$ + asymptotic flatness; Schwarzschild as unique vacuum limit).

**Standing prohibition:** The UDT metric is **not** an ansatz. Do not use ansatz framing.

Cross-references: CG §1.0 (derivation chain).

### §1.2 D1 cosmological boundary condition

**Status:** CLOSED at canonical content. $\Delta\phi = 7.003$ is a **global geometric boundary condition** fixed by an algebraic chain — not sourced from microphysics or particle counting.

**Algebraic chain:**

$$\text{CMB redshift } z = 1100 \;\Longrightarrow\; \phi(r_*) = \ln(1101) = 7.003974$$

**Misner-Sharp mass relation:**

$$e^{-2\phi(r_*)} = 1 - \frac{2GM}{c^2 r_*}$$

**Self-referential closure of the universe:**

$$c^2 = \frac{2GM}{r_*}$$

**Numerical verification:** < 0.01% relative error using BAO parameters $\mu_g = 0.2473$ Gpc⁻¹ and $r_*^{\rm cosmo} = 9.16$ Gpc.

**Discipline:** Do not attempt to source $\Delta\phi = 7.003$ from particle counting or ODE integration; it is required by the mass-volume relation. The ODE question (profile shape $\phi(r)$) is separately validated.

Cross-references: CG §1.0 (metric); CG §12 (cosmological cavity context).

### §1.3 Branch-M canonical anchor

**Locked vacuum** at the micro-scale hadronic cavity:

| Quantity | Value |
|---|---|
| Central depth | $\phi_0 = -\cos(\pi/5) = -0.809$ |
| Effective screening mass-squared | $\mu^2 = \pi/3$ |
| Outer cavity scale | $r_* = 6.9875$ natural units ($= 7 - 1/80$) |
| Sub-barrier electron mode | $E_1 = 2\sqrt{2}/3$ |

**Numerical confirmation:** CR-417 / Session 45 §230 G3 at $1.5 \times 10^{-5}$ relative error.

**Branch character:** Frobenius-irregular central depth. Outer Neumann BC $G'(r_*) = 0$. Homogeneous nonlinear screened Klein-Gordon $\Box_g\phi - \mu^2\phi = 0$ constraint.

Cross-references: CG §25 (Two-Branch Ontology Phase A.3); CG §13 (lepton mass context).

### §1.4 Branch-C canonical anchor — two role-distinct canonical scaffolds

Two **structurally distinct canonical objects** carry Branch-C cosmological cavity content at different structural roles. Both produce $\phi(r_{\rm CMB}) = \ln(1101) = 7.003974$ at the outer cavity anchor; both are canonical at CG. They are **not two hypotheses about one scaffold's evolution** — they are two canonical objects whose roles do not overlap.

**S64-003 (H1) evolved-form / (H2) distinct-family hypothesis framing RETRACTED at canonical-record scope (S65-002 dispatch landing, 2026-05-14).** Reframe driven by S65-001 PONDER side-effect findings S9.1 + S9.3 + Verifier-α S-Vα-4 cross-reference sharpening. Per CG §12.7 line 1645 + §12.12.19/§12.12.20 verbatim: the two scaffolds carry **different canonical-content properties** (algebraic-determination vs empirical-coefficient nature) and **occupy different structural roles** (algebraic-bridge vs Einstein-closing matter scaffold) — they are not parameterized refinements of each other.

#### §1.4.1 Canonical algebraic-bridge form (CG §25.3 / §12.7 polynomial)

**Structural role:** Algebraic-bridge content. Carries the canonical link between Branch-M angular sector and Branch-C cosmological scaffold via the Diophantine triple $(j, \ell, |\kappa_{\max}|) = (1/2, 1, 3)$ and the reciprocal-pair constraint $ac = 1$ (§1.7 below; archived VR §256). Provides the canonical screening-mass bridge $\mu_g = \pi\sqrt{\pi/3}/13$.

$$\phi_{\rm bridge}(r) \;=\; \mu_g r\left[\frac{3}{2} - \cos\!\left(\frac{\pi}{5}\right)\mu_g r + \frac{2}{3}\mu_g^2 r^2\right] \;=\; \frac{3}{2}\mu_g r - \cos\!\left(\frac{\pi}{5}\right)\mu_g^2 r^2 + \frac{2}{3}\mu_g^3 r^3$$

with parameters:

| Quantity | Value |
|---|---|
| Inverse scale | $\mu_g = \pi\sqrt{\pi/3}/13 \approx 0.2473$ Gpc⁻¹ |
| Outer scale | $r_{\rm CMB} = 9.164$ Gpc |
| Outer anchor | $\phi(r_{\rm CMB}) = \ln(1101) = 7.003974$ |

**Canonical properties** (per CG §25.3 + §12.7):
- Coefficients $(3/2, -\cos(\pi/5), 2/3)$ are **algebraically determined** by the Diophantine triple + reciprocal-pair constraint $ac = 1$. Zero free parameters.
- $\phi_{\rm bridge}(0) = 0$; $\phi_{\rm bridge}'(0) = (3/2)\mu_g \ne 0$ — **Frobenius-irregular at $r = 0$** (the linear $(3/2)\mu_g r$ term is forbidden by the indicial equation at a regular origin; CG §12.7 line 1644, CR-408 sharpened).
- **NOT a regular-origin vacuum solution at any $\phi_0$**; **does not satisfy the homogeneous screened KG equation** with $\mu_g$ (A3-G1 evidence chain at CG §25.6).

**Used at:** S58–S63 numerical anchors invoking the $\mu_g$ bridge value; cosmological calibration; Diophantine-uniqueness theorem A.3.T6 substrate.

**Canonical homes:** CG §25.3 (algebraic-bridge theorem A.3.T3) + CG §12.7 (geometric polynomial coefficients + algebraic-determination derivation chain).

#### §1.4.2 Canonical Einstein-closing matter scaffold (N=2 regular-origin)

**Structural role:** Einstein-closing matter scaffold. Closes the full Einstein system on UDT metric with all gates passing (positivity, Bianchi, Misner-Sharp). Per CG §12.12.20 + CR-413/414/414b/415/416 substrate: the metric-determined closure shows the inferred "$T^\mu{}_\nu$" is identically $G^\mu{}_\nu/(8\pi G)$ — Einstein-tensor arithmetic, not physical matter content.

$$\phi_{\rm matter}(r) \;=\; a_2\,r^2 \;+\; a_3\,r^3$$

**Canonical properties** (per CG §12.7 line 1645 + §12.12.19/§12.12.20):
- Coefficients $a_2, a_3$ are **BC + BS-determined empirical (basis-dependent) coefficients**. Algebraic-determination via Diophantine triple does **NOT** apply to this scaffold (algebraic-determination property belongs to §1.4.1 algebraic-bridge form).
- $\phi_{\rm matter}(0) = 0$; $\phi_{\rm matter}'(0) = 0$ — **Frobenius-regular at $r = 0$**.
- **Cleaner physical-matter properties** than §1.4.1 form; closes Einstein-tensor arithmetic at machine precision ($1.25 \times 10^{-16}$ relative residual per CR-413/414b/416; CG §12.12.20).
- **Ansatz-conditional on D-POLY-1** (CG §22.5 item 12 / active doc §3.4): polynomial form itself is not metric-forced.

**Used at:** Einstein-system-closing matter-scaffold work where regular-origin behavior at $r = 0$ is required (positivity, Bianchi, Misner-Sharp gates); variational closure work where self-adjointness needs regular-origin.

**Canonical homes:** CG §12.12.19 (regular-origin scaffold + full-Einstein EOS structure, CR-408 / CR-412, Session 16) + CG §12.12.20 (metric-determined closure, CR-413 through CR-416). **N=2 canonical coefficients $(a_2, a_3) = (0.03156295029608829, 0.005656770825770722)$ at $r_{\rm CMB} = 9.164$ Gpc, $\phi(R_{\rm CMB}) = \ln 1101 = 7.00397413672268$ are at IH §47 line 5964** (Session 17 Priority 1 Action-Principle Investigation; canonical CR-412 numerical pinning verbatim). CG §12.7 line 1645 carries the status-note linkage between the algebraic-bridge form (§1.4.1) and the matter scaffold (§1.4.2). [Substrate citation corrected at S71-001a edit (i), 2026-05-17 evening, per S70-005 Vα-Sα-1 — prior "IH §49.2" attribution mislabel; IH §49.2 is Pre-2BO CMB Projection Machinery, not the N=2 numerical anchor.]

#### §1.4.3 Operational distinction (role-distinct canonical objects)

The two scaffolds are **structurally distinct canonical objects at different roles**:

| Property | §1.4.1 algebraic-bridge form | §1.4.2 Einstein-closing matter scaffold |
|---|---|---|
| Role | Algebraic-bridge content (Branch-M ↔ Branch-C via canonical triple) | Einstein-system closure on UDT metric (positivity + Bianchi + Misner-Sharp) |
| Leading term | $(3/2)\mu_g r$ (linear) | $a_2 r^2$ (quadratic) |
| Origin behavior | Frobenius-IRREGULAR ($\phi'(0) \ne 0$) | Frobenius-REGULAR ($\phi'(0) = 0$) |
| Coefficient determination | Algebraically determined via Diophantine triple + $ac = 1$ | Empirical (basis-dependent) |
| Homogeneous screened KG | Does NOT satisfy (A3-G1 evidence) | Closes full Einstein system at $T^\mu{}_\nu \equiv G^\mu{}_\nu / (8\pi G)$ |
| Canonical home | CG §25.3 + §12.7 | CG §12.12.19 + §12.12.20 (N=2 numerical anchor IH §47 line 5964); CG §12.7 line 1645 status-note linkage |

The two scaffolds do not "evolve into" each other and are not parameterized refinements of a single scaffold. Each is canonical at its own structural role; the other-role canonical object is not its alternate-form.

#### §1.4.4 Operational discipline at dispatch design

Dispatches invoking Branch-C scaffold content must **specify which role-form is invoked**:

- **Algebraic-bridge content** (Diophantine triple selection, screening-mass bridge $\mu_g$, A.3.T6 uniqueness, lepton-mass-formula angular factors $(2\ell+1)/(2j+1)$): use §1.4.1 algebraic-bridge form.
- **Einstein-closing matter scaffold content** (variational closure work where self-adjointness needs regular-origin; full-Einstein gates verification; matter-scaffold construction at canonical metric-determined closure): use §1.4.2 N=2 regular-origin scaffold.
- **Form-T mode-finding at Branch-C** (Dirac eigenvalue problems, $(G^2+F^2)$ envelope analysis, α-derivation work, sub-leading WKB error-bound machinery): **PIN §1.4.2 N=2 regular-origin scaffold**. §1.4.1 algebraic-bridge form is Frobenius-irregular at origin (per CG §12.7 line 1704: "$\phi'(0) = (3/2)\mu_g \ne 0$ ... WKB-type envelope valid for $r \gtrsim 0.5$ Gpc, not a regular-origin solution"); Form-T eigenmode integration from regular-origin BC requires Frobenius-regular $\phi(r)$ at origin so the spin-connection $\pm\phi'$ couples regularly with the Frobenius indices of $(G, F)$. **NEW S68-002 operational discipline (SE-S68-001-1, 2026-05-15):** future Form-T mode-finding work at Branch-C must explicitly pin §1.4.2 N=2 substrate; §1.4.1 is NOT the canonical Form-T mode-finding substrate (this resolves the S61-006 → active doc §2.3 → SE-S67-004-2 inheritance-chain mislabel propagated through SESSION68_PROMPT.md line 46).
- **L3 (MF) coupled-system on-shell closure test charter** (S65-003 candidate): selects per coupling regime; charter sub-choice pinning required per F-candidate-S63-002-a preventive-discipline pattern.
- **L1 (MD) joint BC derivation** (S65-001): operated against the canonical action structure at §8.5.1 with both forms operationally available at canonical content; outer-boundary BC structure factorization holds for either scaffold (S65-001 PONDER §5).

Cross-references: CG §25.3 (algebraic-bridge theorem A.3.T3); CG §12.7 (geometric polynomial coefficients); CG §12.12.19/§12.12.20 (Einstein-closing matter scaffold canonical-record summary); **IH §47 line 5964 (N=2 numerical anchor: $(a_2, a_3) = (0.03156295029608829, 0.005656770825770722)$ at $r_{\rm CMB} = 9.164$ Gpc, $\phi_{\rm target} = 7.00397413672268$; corrected at S71-001a edit (i) per S70-005 Vα-Sα-1; prior "IH §49.2" was section-attribution mislabel)**; §1.6 above (frame-relation $C_\ell^{\rm UDT}(r)$ uses $\phi_0(r)$ — which role-form is invoked at numerical application is a per-dispatch sub-choice); §1.7 below (Pell triple substrate uses §1.4.1 algebraic-bridge form); §3.2 D-COMP-MATTER-L1 (joint BC derivation operates against either scaffold per S65-001 §5.2); IH §49.10 §5.5 L1 forward-arc + IH §49.10 §5.6 L3 forward-arc (substantive Phase 2 dispatches select per coupling regime; §5 retired to IH §49.10 at S74-005).

### §1.4.5 The absolute cosmological scale is one irreducible input (the Eddington-Dirac large number) — S109

**Canonical statement.** The absolute cosmological length scale — equivalently the cosmic mass $M$, the particle count $N = M/m_p$, or the micro→macro reflexive ratio $\Lambda = r_{\rm CMB}/r_*^{\rm phys} \approx 1.1\times10^{38}$ — is **one irreducible observational input**. It is NOT derivable from $ds^2$ + the locked dimensionless parameters $\{\phi_0=-\cos(\pi/5),\ \mu^2=\pi/3,\ r_*=6.9875\}$ + lab anchors. The S109 four-dispatch scale arc established this by the following chain:

- **DERIVED (micro scale):** the $m_e$ lab anchor ($C = m_e/E_1$, $E_1 = 2\sqrt2/3$) fixes the micro length unit ($1$ natural length $= E_1\lambda_e \approx 364$ fm), pinning the Branch-M cavity $r_*^{\rm phys}\approx 2.5$ pm.
- **DERIVED (dimensionless cosmological structure):** the boundary condition $\phi(r_{\rm CMB}) = \ln 1101$ [from the $T_{\rm CMB}$ observation] fixes only the dimensionless product $\mu_g\,r_{\rm CMB} = 2.266$.
- **SCALE-COVARIANT (no absolute length):** $ds^2$ (the flux/φ system is invariant under $(r,\mu)\to(\lambda r,\,\mu/\lambda)$; the only invariant is the dimensionless $\mu r$) AND the Misner-Sharp self-closure $c^2 = 2GM/r_{\rm CMB}$ (the MS mass $M(r)=(c^2 r/2G)(1-e^{-2\phi})$ is profile-defined; the closure is auto-satisfied at *any* absolute $r_{\rm CMB}$ as a consequence of the near-horizon boundary condition $e^{-2\phi(r_{\rm CMB})}=1/1101^2\approx0$) are BOTH scale-covariant — neither fixes the absolute scale.
- **INTENSIVE-not-EXTENSIVE (angular Diophantine):** the angular Diophantine triple $(j,\ell,|\kappa_{\max}|)=(1/2,1,3)$ fixes the *intensive* structure (su(3) closure on $S^2$, $|\kappa|\le 3$ selection, particle types) but NOT the *extensive* count $N\sim10^{80}$. $N$ is not a clean power of $\Lambda$ ($p = \log N/\log\Lambda = 2.104$) nor a clean function of $\alpha_G$ (the closest, $N\sim(1/\alpha_G^{\rm proton})^2$, is off by $\sim4000\times$) — it is the **Eddington-Dirac large number**, which no theory (UDT or ΛCDM) derives from first principles.

**Consequence.** Canonical UDT derives the micro physics, the dimensionless cosmological structure $\mu_g r_{\rm CMB}=2.266$, and the particle types, and requires **exactly ONE cosmological input — the absolute scale** — on equal footing with all of physics (Theory Rule 5 permits direct observations for precisely this role). This **resolves D-UNIT-CONV-1 / D-AA-GAP-1** (CG §22.5 #31/#33): the "observational-anchor closure path" is not a pending derivation but the necessary single input. It also resolves the 71.886 thread — CR-399's 71.886 was empirically anchored (fit) precisely *because* this one number is irreducible (D-71886-REEXAMINE-1; the per-mode alignment factor scatters 71.6–76.2, the fingerprint of a fit, and 54 closed-form candidates failed).

**Cross-references:** S109 dispatches `dispatch_D_CMB_PATTERN_SCALE_1/`, `dispatch_D_71886_REEXAMINE_1/`, `dispatch_D_UNIT_CONV_1/`, `dispatch_D_MODECOUNT_N_1/` (each `AUDIT.md`); CG §22.5 #31 (D-UNIT-CONV-1) + #33 (D-AA-GAP-1); §1.3 (Branch-M micro anchor) + §1.4 (Branch-C macro anchor); §1.6.5 (the clustering-scale absolute normalization = this input).

### §1.5 Two-Branch Ontology (canonical reference)

Two branches **unified at metric level** (single canonical UDT metric) and **distinguished at constraint-package level**. No shared spacetime region; no three-regime transition zone (spatial-junction framing retracted per A.3.T4).

**Canonical home:** CG §25 (Two-Branch Ontology Phase A.3, Session 24). Includes Theorems A.3.T1 through A.3.T6, closures D-A3-1/2/3, evidence gates A3-G1/G2/G3.

Branch-M = hadronic cavity (§1.3 above). Branch-C = cosmological cavity (§1.4 above). Algebraic linkage at CG §25.3.

### §1.6 Frame-relation closure (canonical $C_\ell$ form) + pure-Bessel kinematic kernel canonicalization (post-S99-009/S99-010)

**Status post-S99-009/S99-010:** CANONICAL at canonical content for **CMB observable scope** via **pure-Bessel kinematic projection**. The §229 frame-relation form stands as the canonical observer-frame line-of-sight identity; the kernel $|K_\ell|^2$ at canonical UDT for CMB observable is the pure-Bessel kinematic projection derived algebraically from $ds^2$ + Tolman + emission model. Operator-class Gate 8 PASS: NO Sturm-Liouville, NO Klein-Gordon, NO screened-KG, NO framework §5 first-order Hamiltonian constraint, NO matter-sector cavity scalar field intermediate.

#### §1.6.1 Frame-relation canonical observer-frame identity (Session 44; archived VR §229; PRESERVED)

Canonical observer-frame line-of-sight $C_\ell$ form derived directly from $ds^2$:

$$C_\ell^{\rm UDT}(r) \;=\; \int_0^{R_{\rm CMB}} dr' \; e^{-3\phi_0(r')} \, |K_\ell(r')|^2 \, P_{\rm src}(r', \ell)$$

with the observer-frame line-of-sight optical-depth measure

$$d\mu_{\rm obs} = e^{-3\phi_0(r)}\,dr, \qquad L_0 = \int_0^{R_{\rm CMB}} e^{-3\phi_0(r)}\,dr = 2.3483\ \text{Gpc}.$$

> **S71-001a edit (iv) precision sharpening (post-S70-005 Vβ-Nβ-1, 2026-05-17 evening):** $L_0 = 2.3483$ Gpc is the 4-sig-fig canonical anchor value on Branch-C §1.4.2 N=2 regular-origin scaffold with canonical coefficients $(a_2, a_3) = (0.03156295029608829, 0.005656770825770722)$ at $r_{\rm CMB} = 9.164$ Gpc, $\phi(R_{\rm CMB}) = \ln 1101$. Archived VR §229.16 "$L_0 \approx 2.347$ Gpc" is 3-sig-fig rounding of the same numerical anchor (not an EPS/method artifact); archived VR is read-only per S64-008 archive-banner convention. Pin 4-sig-fig $L_0 = 2.3483$ Gpc at all numerical execution work on Branch-C §1.4.2 dipole-class observables.

> **S99-009 independent cross-check (2026-05-26):** $L_{\rm eff,B} = \int_0^{r_{\rm CMB}} e^{-3\phi_0(r)}\,dr = 2.348$ Gpc reproduced at sub-permille agreement with the canonical $L_0 = 2.3483$ Gpc anchor (and archived VR §65 $\approx 2.347$ Gpc 3-sig-fig rounding) via independent pure-Bessel inversion machinery on canonical Branch-C N=2 substrate. Sympy-verified $\sqrt{-g}$ φ-independence ($\det g = -c^2 r^4 \sin^2\theta$ exact simplification; the $e^{-2\phi}$ and $e^{2\phi}$ cancel).

#### §1.6.2 UDT-native radial-correlation form $P_\rho^\ell(r_1, r_2)$ — canonical CMB observable form (CANONICALIZED at D-PRHO-ELL-NATIVE-1; Gate 10 SCAFFOLDING flag LIFTED)

**Status:** CANONICAL CONTENT post-D-PRHO-ELL-NATIVE-1 (2026-05-28). The UDT-native radial-correlation form is derived at canonical content (canonical static metric + canonical Tolman + angular isotropy at fixed shell — NOT 3D-Fourier-isotropy). The S99-013 Gate 10 SCAFFOLDING flag is LIFTED at H_RADIAL_A landing (Thrust A canonicalization SUCCEEDED at sympy machine precision); pre-D-PRHO-ELL-NATIVE-1 Gate 10 hidden-assumption historical content migrated to IH §50.16.F.

**Canonical CMB observable form:**

$$\boxed{\;C_\ell^{TT} \;=\; \int_0^{r_{\rm CMB}} dr_1 \int_0^{r_{\rm CMB}} dr_2 \;\mathcal{W}^{TT}(r_1)\,\mathcal{W}^{TT}(r_2)\,P_\rho^\ell(r_1, r_2)\;}$$

with:

- $\mathcal{W}^{TT}(r) = r^2 \cdot e^{-3\phi_0(r)}$ — canonical radial weight (preserved derivation chain)
- $P_\rho^\ell(r_1, r_2) = \langle \rho_{\ell m}(r_1)\,\rho_{\ell m}^*(r_2)\rangle$ — angular-decomposed two-point cosmic matter correlation between radial shells, under angular isotropy at fixed shell

The UDT-native form accommodates **observer-centric radial structure** in the cosmic matter distribution: $P_\rho^\ell(r_1, r_2)$ may depend on $r_1, r_2$ separately, NOT only on Bessel-decomposed translation-invariant kernel. This is the Gate 10 distinction from LCDM (which forces statistical homogeneity in flat 3-space via single global $P(k)$).

**Derivation chain (algebraic; sympy-verified at canonical content; NO wave equation):**

1. **Coordinate volume element from $\sqrt{-g}$** (sympy-verified $\sqrt{-g} = c\,r^2\,|\sin\theta|$ — φ-independent): radial Jacobian for shell-of-radius-$r$ is $r^2$.
2. **Tolman temperature redshift** (Tolman 1934 + canonical static metric; observer at origin where $\phi(0) = 0$): $T_{\rm obs}(r)/T_{\rm src}(r) = e^{-\phi(r)}$.
3. **Surface brightness in static metric** for thermal radiation: $I_{\rm obs}/I_{\rm src} = (T_{\rm obs}/T_{\rm src})^4 = e^{-4\phi(r)}$.
4. **Fractional temperature observable** $\delta T_{\rm obs}/T_{\rm obs}$ (the Planck-reported quantity) absorbs one power of $e^{+\phi}$ in observer-frame normalization at linearization.
5. **Net radial weight:** $\mathcal{W}^{TT}(r) = r^2 \cdot e^{-3\phi_0(r)}$.
6. **Angular decomposition** $\delta\rho(r, \theta, \phi) = \sum_{\ell m} \rho_{\ell m}(r) Y_{\ell m}(\theta, \phi)$ + **angular isotropy at fixed shell** $\langle \rho_{\ell m}(r_1)\,\rho_{\ell' m'}^*(r_2)\rangle = \delta_{\ell\ell'}\,\delta_{mm'}\,P_\rho^\ell(r_1, r_2)$ → canonical UDT-native observable form.

This matches the canonical $e^{-3\phi_0}$ LOS measure used in archived VR §65 + §80 + §229.4 + §82.4. The factor 3 (not 4) derivation is per §229.4. The angular-isotropy-at-fixed-shell assumption is **vastly weaker** than the LCDM 3D-Fourier-isotropy assumption — it requires statistical isotropy on angular variables at each radial shell only, NOT statistical homogeneity in flat 3-space.

> #### §1.6.2.8 ★ The temperature observable is INCOMPLETE — the intrinsic re-emergence term (DERIVED; D-CMB-EE-PROJECTION-SPIN-1, S116, 2026-06-03)
>
> **The `δT/T = −δφ` relation used above (steps 2–5, the Tolman/Sachs-Wolfe gravitational *redshift*) is only HALF of the temperature.** It is the analog of ΛCDM's Sachs-Wolfe $\Phi$ term, which dominates only the low-ℓ plateau. The CMB is the **re-emergence of recycled matter as radiation** (AR §1.9 recycling ontology), and a denser re-emergence region is intrinsically **hotter** — so there is an **intrinsic emission-temperature term** that the SW-only model omitted (the analog of ΛCDM's $\tfrac14\delta_\gamma$, which *dominates* at the acoustic peaks). The complete temperature is:
> $$\boxed{\;\frac{\delta T}{T} \;=\; \underbrace{-\delta\phi}_{\text{SW redshift}} \;+\; \underbrace{\tfrac14\,\frac{\delta\rho}{\rho}}_{\text{intrinsic re-emergence temp}}\;}$$
> **Both terms DERIVED, the coefficient is NOT free:**
> - **c = ¼ from Stefan-Boltzmann** — $\rho_\gamma \propto T^4 \Rightarrow \delta\rho_\gamma/\rho_\gamma = 4\,\delta T/T$. This is the **canonical UDT blackbody** (the Planck spectrum UDT already derives), not an import.
> - **$\delta\rho$ from the metric's own Einstein tensor** ($\rho = -G^t{}_t/8\pi G$, linearized in the breathing $\delta\phi$ *with angular dependence kept* — sympy-verified): $\delta\rho = -\frac{1}{8\pi G r^2}\partial_\theta^2\delta\phi + \frac{e^{-2\phi_0}}{4\pi G r}\partial_r\delta\phi + (\dots)\delta\phi$. The angular-Laplacian coefficient $-1/(8\pi G r^2) \neq 0$ ⇒ for a mode $Y_{\ell m}$, **$\delta\rho \to +\frac{\ell(\ell+1)}{8\pi G r^2}\,\delta\phi$** at the acoustic scales — the density carries the angular $\ell(\ell+1)$ (a tidal/Laplacian object, like EE's $\eth^2$).
> - **Background:** $B \equiv 8\pi G r^2\rho_0 = [2r\phi_0' + e^{2\phi_0} - 1]e^{-2\phi_0} = 1.0000$ at $r_{\rm CMB}$ (deep-boundary limit $e^{2\phi_0}e^{-2\phi_0}=1$). So $\delta\rho/\rho = \ell(\ell+1)\delta\phi/B \approx \ell(\ell+1)\delta\phi$, and the SW↔intrinsic transition is at $\ell(\ell+1)=4B \Rightarrow \ell\approx2$: **the intrinsic term dominates TT at all observable ℓ; the SW $-\delta\phi$ is only an $\ell\approx2$ correction.** So TT traces the **breathing density** ($\delta T/T \approx \tfrac14\,\delta\rho/\rho$, the $\tfrac14\delta_\gamma$ analog).
>
> **Consequence — this fixes the S115 EE-amplitude "overshoot" (which was a TT base-model artifact, not an EE failure):** with TT $\sim$ density (tidal, $\ell(\ell+1)$) instead of the bare potential, and EE $= \eth^2(\text{velocity}) \sim \ell(\ell+1)\times$velocity, the **$C_\ell^{EE}/C_\ell^{TT}$ ratio collapses from $\ell^4$ to $\ell^0$** (validated: log-log slope $+4.04 \to +0.04$ with a realistic source). The "metric over-predicts EE small-scale power by 2×" finding (S115 E6 / AR §1.9.3) was an artifact of truncating $\delta T/T$ to the Sachs-Wolfe redshift piece.
>
> **STATUS — MECHANISM DERIVED; full quantitative Planck match PENDING.** Derived: $\delta\rho$ carries $\ell(\ell+1)$ (G^t_t, sympy); $c=\tfrac14$ (blackbody); the $\ell^4\to\ell^0$ collapse. **Caveat (not fully forced):** the radiation-tracks-density link $\delta\rho_\gamma/\rho_\gamma = \delta\rho/\rho$ (re-emerged radiation contrast = breathing density contrast) is physically motivated (radiation re-emerges $\propto$ local dissolution) → $c=\tfrac14\,\eta$ with tracking $\eta\sim1$; the $\ell^2$-fix is independent of $\eta$. **Open:** the full forward model (comb + the *mild* velocity transfer $\omega(\ell)\sim\ell^{-0.2}$, consistent with the S115 ℓ(ℓ+1)-careful transfer) reproducing the peak-by-peak TT+EE+TE; the proper Planck fit was not yet achieved. Cross-ref: `dispatch_D_CMB_EE_PROJECTION_SPIN_1/AUDIT.md` (full S116 arc + scripts `derive_intrinsic_coeff.py`, `density_angular_test.py`, `tt_density_term.py`, `complete_model_vs_planck.py`, `full_forward_firewall.py`).

**LCDM-isotropy reduction reference (`# SCAFFOLDING:` flagged):**

Under explicit LCDM-isotropy assumption — single $P(k)$ for cosmic matter at all radial distances; flat 3-space Fourier basis; statistical isotropy of $\delta\rho_k$ in $\hat{k}$ direction — the UDT-native form reduces to the Bessel/P(k) form:

$$P_\rho^\ell\big|_{\rm LCDM}(r_1, r_2) \;=\; \frac{2}{\pi}\int dk\,k^2\,P(k)\,j_\ell(k r_1)\,j_\ell(k r_2) \quad\text{`# SCAFFOLDING: LCDM cosmological-isotropy reduction`}$$

$$C_\ell^{TT}\big|_{\rm LCDM} \;=\; \frac{2}{\pi}\int dk\,k^2\,P(k)\,|\Delta_\ell(k)|^2, \quad \Delta_\ell(k) = \int_0^{r_{\rm CMB}} dr \, \mathcal{W}^{TT}(r) \, j_\ell(kr)$$

The Bessel/P(k) form is canonical content ONLY UNDER explicit LCDM-isotropy reduction. **At canonical UDT, the PRIMARY form is the radial-correlation form above; the Bessel/P(k) form is the LCDM-reduction reference.** The relaxation lifted at the UDT-native canonicalization is "radial translation invariance under flat 3-space Fourier basis" — that's the load-bearing LCDM-borrowed assumption that the canonical UDT framework does NOT make.

**Substantive content of the canonicalization (per D-PRHO-ELL-NATIVE-1 Thrust B):** ℓ-structure of $C_\ell^{TT}$ comes from DIFFERENT sources in the two forms. In the LCDM-Bessel form, ℓ-structure is INHERITED from the kernel $j_\ell(kr)$ (assumption-derived from flat-3-space-Fourier basis). In the UDT-native form, ℓ-structure comes EXCLUSIVELY from $P_\rho^\ell$ ℓ-dependence. At ℓ-flat $g_\ell = 1$ pinning of $P_\rho^\ell$, the UDT-native form predicts ℓ-flat $C_\ell^{TT}$ — no Bessel-kernel ℓ-shape. The observed CMB ℓ-structure must come from explicit ℓ-shape in $P_\rho^\ell$, i.e. from the postulated cosmic matter distribution's angular-decomposed radial correlation (§1.6.5 forward-prediction class).

#### §1.6.2.7 Canonical-content constraints on $P_\rho^\ell(r_1, r_2)$ (NEW post-D-PRHO-ELL-NATIVE-1)

The UDT-native form admits the following canonical-content constraints on $P_\rho^\ell$:

1. **Positivity at single shell**: $P_\rho^\ell(r, r) \ge 0$ for all $r \in [0, r_{\rm CMB}]$ and $\ell \ge 0$ (from $|\rho_{\ell m}(r)|^2 \ge 0$)
2. **Symmetry**: $P_\rho^\ell(r_1, r_2) = P_\rho^\ell(r_2, r_1)$ (from real δρ)
3. **Cauchy-Schwarz**: $|P_\rho^\ell(r_1, r_2)|^2 \le P_\rho^\ell(r_1, r_1) \cdot P_\rho^\ell(r_2, r_2)$ (positive-semi-definite quadratic form)
4. **Positive-semi-definite integral operator**: $C_\ell^{TT} \ge 0$ for any admissible $P_\rho^\ell$ paired with canonical $\mathcal{W}^{TT}$
5. **T5 invariance (optional canonical content from LAYER 3)**: $P_\rho^\ell(r_*(r_1), r_*(r_2)) = P_\rho^\ell(r_1, r_2)$ where $r_*(r)$ is the canonical T5 partner-mapping (canonical content at full-φ(r)-profile layer per D-CROSS-SCALE-SYMMETRY-1)
6. **Observer-centric radial structure permitted**: $P_\rho^\ell(r_1, r_2)$ may depend on $r_1, r_2$ separately — this is the canonical UDT distinction from LCDM (under LCDM-isotropy, constraint (6) is RELAXED to "radial translation invariance under flat 3-space Fourier basis")

Constraints (1)-(4) are structural. Constraint (5) is optional canonical content depending on the LAYER 3 status carried-forward from D-CROSS-SCALE-SYMMETRY-1 + D-T5-CMB-FORWARD-1. Constraint (6) is the canonical UDT distinction from LCDM.

### §1.6.5 Boundary matter distribution postulate — structural-object features as forward-testable falsifiable prediction (NEW post-S99-010)

> **★ DEMOTED at S105 (2026-05-29; Charles-authorized) — the matter-clustering source is FALSIFIED.** S104 found that real cosmic structure shows ONE BAO bump (~150 Mpc), not seven peaks, and the measured rms contrast σ(R) at the §1.6.5 scales (14–131 Mpc) is **70–640× larger** than the ~0.114% the CMB needs; a static universe has no early-smoothness rescue. D-CMB-ANGULAR-PATTERN-1 (S105) then showed the S103 "7/7 Planck TT peaks reproduced" result was **source-driven (this falsified §1.6.5 structure) + convention-driven (thin-shell $L_\ell=\pi r_{\rm CMB}/\ell$), 0% geometry-driven**: canonical UDT's actual smooth thermal source through the canonical geometric kernel predicts a **peakless** angular spectrum (CG §11.9 Priority-2 addendum). **This §1.6.5 postulate is retained as historical record but is NOT canonical-content load-bearing for the CMB anisotropy.** The peak question stays OPEN ("keep searching," Charles 2026-05-29) — geometric and EM-channel routes under investigation. The text below is preserved per leave-behind-not-delete; read it as the falsified-source record, not active canonical content.

**Status post-S99-010 (SUPERSEDED — see S105 demotion banner above):** CANONICAL POSTULATE at canonical content. Forward-testable falsifiable prediction class per framework §14.1 P5 (DES / KiDS / DESI DR2+ / LSST / Euclid future-survey cross-correlation).

**Canonical UDT boundary matter distribution postulate:** The boundary matter distribution at $r_{\rm CMB} = 9.164$ Gpc on canonical Branch-C N=2 substrate has **discrete structural-object features at characteristic clustering scales matching observed Planck CMB peak positions** $[220, 545, 810, 1140, 1430, 1740, 2050]$, which project to physical scales at the boundary via the **angular-size convention** $L_\ell \approx \pi r_{\rm CMB} / \ell$ (this is the convention that makes the BAO kaleidoscope reading at S99-007 self-consistent at 13% match between UDT ℓ=220 → 131 Mpc and LCDM BAO 150 Mpc):

| Planck peak $\ell$ | Physical scale at boundary $L_\ell = \pi r_{\rm CMB}/\ell$ |
|---|---|
| 220 | **131 Mpc** (BAO-adjacent; LCDM BAO 150 Mpc within 13% kaleidoscope match) |
| 545 | **53 Mpc** |
| 810 | **36 Mpc** |
| 1140 | **25 Mpc** |
| 1430 | **20 Mpc** |
| 1740 | **17 Mpc** |
| 2050 | **14 Mpc** |

**Postulated boundary inhomogeneity amplitude:** $\sigma_{\delta\rho/\bar\rho} \sim 0.1\text{–}1\%$ at canonical content. Cross-pipeline-consistent across:

- S99-006 cavity-field inversion (sub-choice A uniform-extended source): $\sigma \sim 0.5\text{–}2\%$ bracket
- S99-007 cross-pipeline bracket (framework §7-§9 inferred-LSS via dipole-anchored conversion): $\sigma \in [0.07, 1.24]\%$
- S99-009 pure-Bessel kinematic inversion: $\sigma = 0.114\%$ (INSIDE framework §7-§9 bracket)
- Charles 6% dipole bracket: $0.114\% \ll 6\%$ (INSIDE)

**This distribution is POSTULATED, not derived from first principles.** Canonical UDT does not solve the chaotic formation of matter distribution from initial conditions (computationally intractable per LCDM precedent — LCDM does not derive structure formation from first principles either; it parametrizes via initial power spectrum + transfer function). The S99-009 pure-Bessel inversion recovered a steep $P(k)$ slope (+71.7 in log-log over 6.7 decades of $k$) which Charles 2026-05-26 catch identified as **"the artifact of using continuous smooth distribution instead of structural-object-aware":** a single continuous power-law $P(k)$ cannot capture discrete clustering at preferred scales corresponding to observed CMB peaks. The structural-object postulate replaces the continuous-$P(k)$ assumption with discrete-feature-at-characteristic-scales for the canonical UDT boundary matter distribution.

**Forward-testable falsifiable prediction (Architecture (A) input per archived VR §228.5):** future sky surveys (DES Y6+, KiDS Final, DESI DR2+, LSST, Euclid) should find matter clustering at structural-object scales $\{131, 53, 36, 25, 20, 17, 14\}$ Mpc with amplitude $\sigma_{\delta\rho/\bar\rho} \sim 0.1\text{–}1\%$. This is a **kaleidoscope-projection prediction**: the same boundary distribution produces observed CMB peaks via §229 + §1.6.2 pure-Bessel kernel AND should be directly detectable in galaxy-survey clustering at boundary-projected angular scales.

**Falsifiability:** If future galaxy surveys find matter clustering at characteristically different scales (significantly outside the postulated $\{131, ..., 14\}$ Mpc set + amplitude bracket $0.1\text{–}1\%$), canonical UDT's boundary matter distribution postulate is REFUTED at canonical content. The postulate is forward-testable in the strong sense.

**What this postulate does NOT do:** It does NOT derive matter clustering from canonical UDT first principles. The static-metric self-consistency derivation of boundary clustering (analogous to LCDM's BAO scale from baryon-photon plasma acoustic oscillations, but at canonical UDT a static-metric derivation — no plasma, no recombination, no expanding universe) is an OPEN canonical-content extension question. It is held in reserve at distinct Charles tier-gate as the "boundary matter clustering question" (open at canonical content post-S99-006 + S99-007 + S99-009 + S99-010); not load-bearing for the structural-object-postulate-as-forward-prediction framing. **S109 resolution (absolute normalization):** the four-dispatch scale arc (D-CMB-PATTERN-SCALE-1 → D-71886-REEXAMINE-1 → D-UNIT-CONV-1 → D-MODECOUNT-N-1; §1.4.5) established that the *absolute* normalization of these scales is one irreducible input (the Eddington-Dirac large number) — the ~150 Mpc clustering scale is not derivable from reservoir dynamics (all canonical reservoir scales are O(Gpc); a single-inhibitor screened reservoir relaxes smooth, a Turing pattern needs un-pinned coefficients), and the apparent $r_{\rm CMB}/71.886$ shortcut is fit, not derived. What remains OPEN is the *dimensionless* structure (the relative spacings $\{131:53:36:\dots\}$); the *absolute* scale is settled as INPUT (§1.4.5).

**Standing discipline (binding post-S99-010; CLAUDE.md "Ontology Discipline" extension):** Future dispatches at CMB observable / polarization / lensing / galaxy-survey-correlation scope use this postulate as canonical input; falsifiability rests with sky survey observations. The postulate's discrete-feature-at-characteristic-scales structure is itself the substantive structural prediction; the smooth-$P(k)$ alternative is identified as scaffolding artifact per Charles 2026-05-26 catch.

#### §1.6.5.1 Canonical-content interpretation: multipole-space peaks NOT real-space correlation peaks (NEW post-D-CMB-DESI-FORWARD-1, 2026-05-28)

The §1.6.5 "discrete structural-object features at characteristic clustering scales" must be interpreted at the **MULTIPOLE-SPACE level** — as peaks in the boundary angular power spectrum $C_\rho^\ell\rvert_{\rm boundary}$ at the convention positions $\ell_n = \pi r_{\rm CMB}/L_n$ (equivalent to real-space angular OSCILLATIONS at characteristic angular scales $\theta_n = L_n/r_{\rm CMB}$). The features are **NOT** to be interpreted as real-space Gaussian peaks in the angular correlation function $\xi(\theta)$ at radii $L_n$. The v1 execution of D-CMB-DESI-FORWARD-1 verified that a Gaussian-peaked $\xi(\theta)$ Legendre-projects to a low-ℓ-dominated smooth angular power spectrum and does NOT reproduce Planck-like discrete multipole peaks at the convention positions. The multipole-space-peak interpretation (v2) preserves canonical-content self-consistency: the UDT-native form (post-D-PRHO-ELL-NATIVE-1) — applied to a multipole-space-peaked $C_\rho^\ell\rvert_{\rm boundary}$ with the §1.6.5 convention peak positions plus the S99-009 amplitude — reproduces the Planck first TT peak at canonical content (D_ℓ peak at $\ell=223$ vs Planck $\ell=220$, within ±50 multipoles).

**Structural clarification:**

- Real-space level: $\xi(\theta)$ has angular OSCILLATIONS at $\theta_n = L_n/r_{\rm CMB}$ (NOT isolated Gaussian peaks).
- Multipole-space level: $C_\rho^\ell\rvert_{\rm boundary}$ has discrete PEAKS at $\ell_n = \pi r_{\rm CMB}/L_n$ corresponding to Planck CMB peak positions $\{220, 545, 810, 1140, 1430, 1740, 2050\}$.
- These two readings are Fourier-Legendre conjugates of the same canonical-content structural-object distribution.

### §1.6.6 Pure-metric polarization observables — projected metric anisotropy in observer tetrad as direction-dependent polarization observable (NEW post-D-CMB-NATIVE-3; FULL-SCOPE CLOSURE post-D-CMB-NATIVE-3-correction)

**Status:** **DERIVED at FULL SCOPE (mechanism + linearity + mode-matching together) post-D-CMB-NATIVE-3-correction (2026-05-28)** + **CANONICAL FORMULA at $(\ell, m)$ basis sum post-D-CMB-NATIVE-4-audit-Q1-sharpening (2026-05-28 late)**. The corrected canonical $C_\ell^{EE}$ formula uses canonical $\mathcal{W}^{EE}_{\rm canonical}(r) = (r_{\rm CMB}-r)/(r_{\rm CMB}\cdot r) \cdot e^{+2\phi_0(r)}$ (three-path-convergent canonical derivation) + Bessel kinematic projection $j_\ell(kr)$ (canonical Q2 derivation at D-CMB-NATIVE-4-audit), replacing both D-CMB-NATIVE-4's ad-hoc $e^{+2\phi_0}$-only form AND D-CMB-NATIVE-4-audit's asserted lensing-kernel form $2r(r_{\rm CMB}-r)/r_{\rm CMB}$. All 15 charter gates from D-CMB-NATIVE-3-correction PASS at machine precision: Σ (sympy identity), T1/T2/S1/P1 (baseline), M1/M2A (signal generation), M3 (mode-matching: frac@ℓ=2 = 1.000, EB ratio ~10³⁰ for both m=1 and m=2), M2B (linearity exponent 1.0000), M4 (active diagnostic), C1 (R_E ~ 2800; D-CMB-NATIVE-2 photon-transport-artifact confirmed at strengthened diagnosis), G1 (prohibited tokens + parallel-transport audit). **Canonical claim (load-bearing):** UDT-native polarization at CMB-class observable scope is the projected metric anisotropy at the observer's tetrad as a function of line-of-sight direction. Not transported field; not photons. The CMB is the angular-anisotropy structure of the observability limit; its polarization is the direction-dependent shape of that limit. Polarization is what detectors register when geometry has direction-dependent anisotropy on the sky.

**Construction (Pass-C lensing-shear analog + canonical $\mathcal{W}^{EE}$ from three-path convergence):**
- $\psi_{\rm lens}(\theta, \phi) = -2 \int_0^{r_{\rm CMB}} dr \cdot \mathcal{W}^{EE}_{\rm canonical}(r) \cdot \delta\phi(r, \theta, \phi)$
- $\boxed{\mathcal{W}^{EE}_{\rm canonical}(r) = (r_{\rm CMB}-r)/(r_{\rm CMB}\cdot r) \cdot e^{+2\phi_0(r)}}$ (D-CMB-NATIVE-4-audit-Q1-sharpening three-path-convergent canonical derivation: Born approximation in canonical UDT static metric + direct projection + Tolman-extension contraindication; CG §12.15.2 factor-by-factor canonical sourcing)
- $\gamma_1 + i\gamma_2 = \eth^2 \psi_{\rm lens}$ (canonical Newman-Penrose ð² operator from CG §12.4; Goldberg convention)
- Explicit form: γ₁ = ∂²_θψ − cot θ · ∂_θψ − csc²θ · ∂²_φψ; γ₂ = (2/sin θ)[∂_θ∂_φψ − cot θ · ∂_φψ]
- **Observer Stokes (CMB convention):** Q ≡ γ₁, **U ≡ −γ₂** (spin-sign-convention bridge: NP ð² is spin-raising so γ₁+iγ₂ is spin +2; CMB Q+iU is spin −2; convention-respecting identification is Q+iU = γ₁−iγ₂); E/B-mode amplitudes via spin-2 SH decomposition.

**Canonical $C_\ell^{EE}$ formula — UDT-native form (CANONICALIZED at D-PRHO-ELL-NATIVE-1 extension; Gate 10 SCAFFOLDING flag LIFTED):**

$$\boxed{\;C_\ell^{EE} \;=\; \frac{(\ell+2)!}{(\ell-2)!} \int_0^{r_{\rm CMB}} dr_1 \int_0^{r_{\rm CMB}} dr_2 \;\mathcal{W}^{EE}(r_1)\,\mathcal{W}^{EE}(r_2)\,P_{\delta\phi}^\ell(r_1, r_2)\;}$$

with:

- $\mathcal{W}^{EE}(r) = (r_{\rm CMB} - r)/(r_{\rm CMB} \cdot r) \cdot e^{+2\phi_0(r)}$ — canonical radial weight (D-CMB-NATIVE-4-audit-Q1-sharpening three-path-convergent canonical derivation; PRESERVED)

- $(\ell+2)!/(\ell-2)!$ — canonical NP ð² spin-2 amplification factor (CG §12.4 + S98-007 sympy-verified at machine precision)

Per D-PRHO-ELL-NATIVE-1 Thrust A canonicalization extension to EE: the UDT-native radial-correlation form is the PRIMARY canonical content; the Bessel/$P_{\delta\phi}(k)$ form is the LCDM-isotropy reduction reference. $$P_{\delta\phi}^\ell\big|_{\rm LCDM}(r_1, r_2) \;=\; \frac{2}{\pi}\int dk\,k^2\,P_{\delta\phi}(k)\,j_\ell(k r_1)\,j_\ell(k r_2) \quad\text{`# SCAFFOLDING: LCDM cosmological-isotropy reduction`}$$

#### §1.6.8 Collective recycling throughput (closed-loop net rate) — operator structure DERIVED, value INPUT (S109)

The closed recycling loop (dissolution at the $\phi=\cos(\pi/5)$ dissolution shell [CG §15.3] → scalar reservoir → re-emergence [CG §18.3a]) has a net mass throughput given by the volume integral of the inter-sector exchange-current divergence — the canonical scalar-tensor non-conservation source $\nabla_\mu T^{\mu\nu}=-(\partial_\phi L)\partial^\nu\phi$ (§1.6.7 Point-1 / CG §18.3a-addendum):
$$\dot M \;=\; \int \nabla_\mu J^\mu\,dV \;=\; 4\pi\int_0^{r_{\rm CMB}} r^2\,\phi_0'(r)\,\rho_{\rm Dirac}(r)\,dr,\qquad \rho_{\rm Dirac}=\langle G^2+F^2\rangle.$$
The integrand $\phi_0'\,(G^2+F^2)$ is the DERIVED full-mass density-channel coupling (§1.6.7 Point-1; the $Ee^{2\phi}GF$ cross-term that cancels in the §4.5b transport identity cancels here too); $r^2\,dr$ is the canonical $\sqrt{-g}$ shell element. **This throughput is the $\nu=r$ (radial, background-gradient $\phi_0'$) face of the inter-sector exchange identity $\nabla_\mu T^{\mu\nu}_{\rm matter}=-(\partial_\phi L)\partial^\nu\phi$; its $\nu=\theta$ (transverse, perturbation-gradient $\partial_\theta\delta\phi$) face is the co-sourced CMB EE polarization current (D-CMB-POL-RECYCLING-CURRENT-1; CG §12.15.6c) — same canonical mechanism, two faces.**

**Steady-state collective rate.** In equilibrium ($\dot M_{\rm diss}=\dot M_{\rm re\text{-}emerge}$, the §107/§33.7 closed-cycle ledger) the characteristic recycling rate per unit mass is the background gradient times the transport speed:
$$\Gamma \;=\; \frac{\dot M}{M} \;\sim\; \langle\phi_0'\rangle\,c_{\rm eff} \;=\; \frac{\langle r\,\phi_0'\rangle}{\tau_{\rm transit}},\qquad \tau_{\rm transit}=\frac{r_{\rm CMB}}{c_{\rm eff}}.$$
**Dimensional form (S109 audit correction):** the dimensionally-consistent rate is $\Gamma\sim\langle\phi_0'\rangle\,c$ (gradient × speed); the bare $\langle\phi_0'\rangle/\tau_{\rm transit}$ has units (length·time)$^{-1}$ and needs a length factor — equivalently $\Gamma\sim\langle r\phi_0'\rangle/\tau_{\rm transit}$ with the dimensionless log-gradient $\langle r\phi_0'\rangle\sim\mu_g r_{\rm CMB}=2.27$. On the Branch-C §1.4.1 background $\langle\phi_0'\rangle\sim\mu_g\approx0.247$ Gpc$^{-1}$:
$$\Gamma\sim\mu_g c\approx 7.6\times10^{-11}\ {\rm yr}^{-1}\ (\tau_\Gamma=\Gamma^{-1}\approx13\ {\rm Gyr}),\qquad \tau_{\rm transit}=r_{\rm CMB}/c\approx30\ {\rm Gyr}$$
— both O(10–30 Gyr), the full-mass recycling cycle (rate gate §1.6.7; RATE_GATE.md), normalized to the total cosmic mass $M=c^2 r_{\rm CMB}/2G\approx1.9\times10^{53}$ kg.

**Inheritance from the absolute-scale input (§1.4.5).** The recycling *timescale* (~10–30 Gyr) is DERIVED **given** the one irreducible absolute-scale input: $\mu_g$ (dimensionful) and $r_{\rm CMB}$ both carry the Gpc unit, so $\tau_{\rm transit}=r_{\rm CMB}/c$ and $\tau_\Gamma=1/(\mu_g c)$ inherit the §1.4.5 input — they are a consequence of {one scale input + the dimensionless structure $\mu_g r_{\rm CMB}=2.266$}, not an independent derivation.

**RATE FROM THE CMB RADIATION FLOW — well-defined up to the radiative efficiency (D-CMB-RATE-BLACKBODY-1, S110; CORRECTED).** A first pass divided the cavity-integrated *reservoir energy* by a residence time and found an 18-order convention spread (recorded below as the superseded reading). **Charles correction (S110): the physical quantity is the radiation FLOW the temperature radiates at us NOW, σT⁴ — a flux, hence a rate by construction — NOT the redshift-stratified reservoir energy.** Recomputed as a flow with the observed local $T_0=2.725$ K: shell $L=4\pi r_{\rm CMB}^2\sigma T_0^4 = 3.1\times10^{48}$ W and volume turnover $L=uVc/r = 4.2\times10^{48}$ W agree to a **factor 4/3** — the 18-order spread was entirely the $e^{4\phi}$ reservoir-framing artifact (the retired "redshifted starlight" ghost; the correct object is the local flow). Equating the radiation flow to the mass-emergence radiative power gives
$$\tau_{\rm recycle} = f\times 1.7\times10^{14}\ {\rm yr},$$
with **$f$ = the radiative efficiency** (fraction of cycled mass-energy emerging as CMB radiation) the *only* remaining freedom. If $f=E_{\rm CMB}/Mc^2=2.3\times10^{-4}$ (radiation lives ~one recycle cycle) then $\tau\approx40$ Gyr $\approx$ the light-crossing time $r_{\rm CMB}/c$ — i.e. the crude $\mu_g c$ estimate (13–30 Gyr) is recovered, no longer a dimensional guess. **Status:** the rate is **well-defined from $T_0$ up to one physical input $f$** (emergence microphysics, not metric-forced); the throughput reading is compatible with §11.9 $W=1$ (internal emergence→dissolution flow, no external leak). $f=2.3\times10^{-4}\to40$ Gyr is **suggestive, not forced** (rests on residence ≈ one cycle). Net: the rate is no longer an 18-order mess; it is one honest input ($f$) away from pinned. Source: `dispatch_D_CMB_RATE_BLACKBODY_1/` (`rate_from_blackbody.py` superseded reservoir pass; flow recompute in S110 record).
> *Superseded reading (reservoir-energy pass):* dividing $E_{\rm CMB}=\int u_{\rm local}\,dV$ (with $T_{\rm local}=T_0e^\phi$, $e^{4\phi}$ boundary-weighted) by a residence time gave $\tau\in[2.45\,{\rm yr},\,4.6\times10^{18}\,{\rm yr}]$ — convention-degenerate. This used the wrong object (stratified reservoir energy, not the local radiation flow); retained only as the record of the misstep.

**Status (S109; consistent with "throughput is an input, not a gap"):**

**Net:** the recycling-flow *structure* (the $\dot M$ integral + the $\Gamma\sim\mu_g c$ rate) is pinned with no new free parameters — the D-CMB-UNIFIED-1 unified-model operators are grounded at the operator/structure level — while the recycling *value/amplitude* and *coherence width* remain HYPOTHESIS-grade INPUT (consistent with D-CMB-UNIFIED-1 §3 labels + the S108 input-class finding). ### §1.7 Pell-DERIVED canonical triple

**Status:** DERIVED at canonical content (Session 58; archived VR §256).

The fundamental Pell solution $(17, 2)$ of $x^2 - 72\,y^2 = 1$ under the change of variables

$$x = 4|\kappa_{\max}| + 5, \qquad y = 2j + 1$$

selects the canonical angular-momentum triple uniquely at $j = 1/2$ Form-T Dirac commitment:

$$(j, \ell, |\kappa_{\max}|) = (1/2, 1, 3)$$

Next Brahmagupta-ladder member $(577, 68) \to (143, 33.5)$ is non-physical. Exhaustive search at $\ell \in \{0, 2, 3, 4, 5\}$ with half-integer $j$ and $K \le 50$: zero additional physical solutions.

**Combinatorial closure of the pion-coefficient identity $84$:**

$$84 \;=\; \binom{2\ell + 2|\kappa_{\max}| + 1}{2\ell + 1} \;=\; \binom{9}{3} \;=\; \dim \operatorname{Sym}^3(\mathbb{R}^7)$$

as bijection cardinality on the κ-orbit (bosonic occupation of $v = 2\ell + 1 = 3$ vector DOFs on $k = 2|\kappa_{\max}| + 1 = 7$-bin orbit; combinatorial closure per CR-A3-T7b).

**Open:** Representation-theoretic content (why this Diophantine identity holds geometrically) is registered as D-A3-2 at §3 (S64-003); canonical home at CG §22.5 item D-A3-2.

Cross-references: archived VR §256 (Pell triple canonical landing); CG §22.5 item D-A3-2 (open structural question); §2 below (Pell-fixed κ orbit invoked at α = +2 verification).

### §1.9 The Unified Recycling Ontology — micro↔macro consilience (histogram-abandoned, breathing-picture; S110)

**What this section is.** A disciplined consolidation, not a new derivation: it states the single ontology that ties the Branch-M micro sector and the Branch-C/CMB macro sector into one picture, and demarcates — line by line — what is DERIVED, what is INPUT by design, what is ASSERTED, and what is OPEN. **Labeling discipline (Charles, S110): when a label is uncertain, default to ASSERTED/HYPOTHESIS, never to DERIVED** (under-claim, never over-claim — the asymmetric cost of the two errors). This section replaces the *static spatial histogram* reading of the CMB anisotropies (closed at S109; DISSOLUTION-MOD-1 + DIFFRACTION-2) with the breathing-picture reading. Every claim below is either a cited forced result or an explicitly-flagged input.

#### §1.9.1 The ontological core — one cavity, two faces

Canonical UDT is a **single static cavity geometry** (the metric §1.1, $\phi_0$-locked vacuum §1.3) hosting an eternal **recycling cycle**: matter dissolves where the local effective $\phi$ crosses the dissolution surface (BH↔hadron, $\phi=0$; CG §15.3, **DERIVED** from the vacuum ODE — eigenvalue spectrum vanishes at $\phi_{0,\rm eff}\to0$) and re-emerges as the cavity reforms (CG §18.3a). The cycle has **two faces**, both projections of the one geometry (Kaleidoscope Principle):

- **Static face (the cavity's matter content):** what the cavity geometry permits to exist — the particle mass spectrum and the light-element partition. **Time-independent; DERIVED** (the temporal "re-emergence" narrative was reframed at the Framing-B retraction, archived VR §31 line 2776 + §47.13 + §62, to *observer-frame static cavity structure*; the operator-level results stand).
- **Dynamic face (the cavity ringing):** the non-static *breathing* $\delta\phi(r,t)$ driven by the ongoing recycling — the source of the CMB anisotropy channel-structure (§1.6.7 + CG §12.15.6b/c). The breathing is what the observed polarization **forces** (§1.9.3).

The throughput **rate** linking the two faces is **INPUT by design** (observation-determined, like ΛCDM's $A_s$; [[feedback_throughput_is_input_not_gap]]; §1.6.8 — the balance $P_{\rm em}=P_{\rm dis}$ is profile-independent/derived, the absolute value is not a derivation target).

#### §1.9.2 The micro face — what re-emerges (DERIVED spectrum + nucleosynthesis floors)

The cavity geometry fixes the matter content with **zero free parameters** beyond the one absolute-scale anchor (§1.4.5):

- **Particle mass ratios — DERIVED, parameter-free** (CG §13.8; arithmetically re-verified S110): $m_p/m_e=6\pi^5=1836.118$ ($-0.0019\%$ vs PDG); $m_\mu/m_e=20\pi^3/3=206.709$ ($-0.029\%$); $m_p/m_\mu=9\pi^2/10$ ($+0.027\%$). No $\phi_0,\mu,r_*,C$ enters.
- **Light-element partition — GEOMETRIC FLOORS** (VR §31; floors, not exact predictions — **stellar genesis adds nucleons on top, so a floor *below* observed is expected and correct**, Charles S110):
  - **He-4:** sub-cavity ratio $r_*/r_b=\varphi_{\rm gold}=(1+\sqrt5)/2$ ($+0.024\%$) $\Rightarrow$ geometric floor $Y_{\rm em}=(r_b/r_*)^3=\sqrt5-2=0.236$ (exact algebraic golden-ratio partition, **DERIVED**); observed $Y_p=0.245$ = floor + stellar increment $\Delta\approx0.009$ (the increment imports standard stellar yields — flagged). The floor sitting $3.6\%$ *below* observed is the prediction, not a miss.
  - **Li-7 — STRUCTURAL resolution (DERIVED-as-absence):** a static cosmology has no hot primordial epoch, so the ΛCDM factor-$\sim3$ Li-7 *over*production simply does not occur (VR §31.13). Robust (an absence argument), and it resolves a standing ΛCDM tension.

## §2. α = +2 baseline — WKB-phase-averaged limit of CG §4.5b canonical transport identity (S68-004 reframe)

**Status (post-S68-004 reframe):** α = +2 is the **canonical WKB-phase-averaged limit** of the exact canonical Form-T transport-identity formula $\alpha_{\rm fit} = 2 + \mathrm{AVG}[(2\kappa/r)(F^2-G^2)/(\phi'(G^2+F^2))]$ now canonically landed at CG §4.5b. **DERIVED at WKB-applicable scope** across all tested substrates (S67-004 BH-branch test profiles + S68-001 canonical Branch-C N=2 + S68-003 canonical Branch-M high-spectrum). Sub-barrier α-deviation IS canonical content via SAME canonical machinery (SE-α-S68-003-1; CG §4.5b unaveraged formula). Promotion path step (iii) CLOSURE-RESHAPED-AT-S68-003 (see §2.5).

**Pre-S68-004 framing (historical):** "DERIVED-at-WKB-leading-order at canonical-content layer; sub-leading WKB error-bound closure for full DERIVED at all canonical-profile regimes OPEN (promotion path step iii)." This framing is **reshaped at canonical content** by SE-α-S68-003-1 — the unaveraged α-formula at CG §4.5b is the exact identity; α = +2 emerges at WKB-applicable scope where the AVG term vanishes.

Canonical home: **CG §4.5b** (S68-004 canonical landing) + **CG §26.5 item (3b)** (S68-004 reframe). Historical source: archived VR §264.11 (S61-005 + S61-006 derivation, which IS the WKB-phase-averaged-limit derivation sharpened at canonical content by SE-α-S68-003-1).

### §2.1 Canonical statement

The canonical Form-T radial equations (CG §4.4) carry a $+\phi'$ diagonal connection coefficient appearing symmetrically in both $G'$ and $F'$ — direct consequence of the canonical tetrad

$$e^a{}_\mu = \mathrm{diag}\!\left(e^{-\phi},\, e^{+\phi},\, r,\, r\sin\theta\right)$$

via the Cartan spin-connection chain.

Multiplying each radial equation by its component and summing: the cross-coupling term $(m\,e^{\phi} + E\,e^{+2\phi})\,GF$ **cancels exactly** (sympy-verified; symbolic coefficient $= 0$, not asymptotic). The residual transport equation is:

$$\boxed{\;\frac{d}{dr}(G^2 + F^2) \;=\; 2\phi'\,(G^2 + F^2) \;+\; \frac{2\kappa}{r}\,(F^2 - G^2)\;}$$

This is an **exact identity** at canonical Form-T (m=0); now canonically landed at CG §4.5b post-S68-004.

**α = +2 canonical reading (S68-004 post-SE-α-S68-003-1 sharpening):** α = +2 is the **WKB-phase-averaged limit** of the exact unaveraged α-formula

$$\alpha_{\rm fit} \;=\; 2 \;+\; \mathrm{AVG}_{\rm fit\,window}\!\left[\frac{(2\kappa/r)(F^2-G^2)}{\phi'(G^2+F^2)}\right]$$

(canonically landed at CG §4.5b). At WKB-oscillatory eigenmodes (classically-allowed region; wavefunction-oscillation-character), $(F^2-G^2)$ oscillates around zero with WKB phase ⇒ AVG ≈ 0 ⇒ $\alpha_{\rm fit} \approx +2$:

$$\langle G^2 + F^2 \rangle \;\propto\; e^{+2\phi} \qquad \Longrightarrow \qquad \boxed{\alpha = +2 \text{ at WKB-applicable scope}}$$

At non-WKB-applicable eigenmodes (sub-barrier OR small-cavity high-|κ|), $(F^2-G^2)$ has near-constant sign ⇒ AVG ≠ 0 ⇒ α deviates predictably via SAME canonical machinery (SE-α-S68-003-1; canonical content per CG §4.5b, NOT outside-scope).

**F131 vigilance check.** The $+\phi'$ diagonal vanishes at the flat-space limit ($\phi \to \mathrm{const} \Rightarrow \alpha = 0$). The result is non-trivially curvature-dependent; not flat-space DOS reproduction.

**SE-9 strengthening at S66-001 (V6 + Verifier-β Nβ-5, 2026-05-14):** the cross-coupling cancellation in $(G^2 + F^2)'$ transport is structural, **not numerical** — sympy exact symbolic residual $= 0$ at gauged Form-T scope (with $E \to E - eA_t(r)$ for any $A_t$ profile). The $(E - eA_t)\,e^{2\phi}$ pieces cancel identically in $GG' + FF'$ leaving $4 m e^\phi GF$ as the only residue (vanishing at $m=0$ canonical Branch-M anchor). The α = +2 canonical Form-T derivation extends to U(1)-gauged Form-T at **exact-identity scope**, regardless of $A_t(r)$ profile. Implication: any future U(1)-gauged extension of α = +2 work can rely on the exact symbolic identity at the canonical Form-T transport-equation level (not per-profile approximation check). Cross-references: `dispatch_S66_001_ponder/PONDER.md` §6 + §10.β Vβ-5; archived VR §264.11 (S61-005 canonical Form-T derivation, ungauged).

### §2.2 Structural decomposition of β

$$\beta_{\rm fit} \;=\; \underbrace{\alpha_{\rm canonical}(+2)}_{\text{profile-universal}} \;+\; \underbrace{(\text{measure Jacobian})(-1)}_{\text{canonical}} \;+\; \underbrace{2 \cdot \left.\frac{d(-\log r)}{d\phi}\right|_{\rm fit-window}}_{\text{profile-and-fit-window-specific}}$$

**Implications:**

- β is a profile-specific canonical-geometry composite.
- α is the profile-universal canonical-content quantity.
- The third (geometric coupling slope) term dominates β's numerical value at typical fit-windows; treating β as profile-universal canonical pinning is F129 at composite level.

**Operational discipline:**

- Per **F132** vigilance: every φ-exponent extraction PONDER §-header must declare whether the target is canonical α (profile-universal) or composite β (profile-specific), and must enumerate the structural decomposition.
- Per **F137** vigilance: Rule 19 universality test must target α-layer, not β-layer, at same precision when both are accessible.

**Sub-leading WKB error-bound closure (historical framing).** If closed at all canonical-profile regimes, α = +2 would promote from DERIVED-at-WKB-leading-order to fully DERIVED at all canonical-profile regimes. **Per S68-004 reframe:** the question's structure is reshaped — α = +2 IS DERIVED at WKB-applicable scope (where it's the canonical prediction); at non-WKB scope it's not "α = +2 with bounded error" but "α = canonical deviation per unaveraged formula" — a different canonical statement.

**S67-004 partial closure status (verifier-sharpened 2026-05-15):** Closure achieved at **massless Form-T spectra** across three test profiles (F1-massless-variant + F2-moderate + F3'-BH-branch-test). IBP bound $|\log U \text{ swing}| \leq 2\max|g/k| + \int|(g/k)'|dr$ with $g = 2\kappa/r$, $k = 2(me^\phi + Ee^{2\phi})$; obs/bound $\in [0.668, 0.824]$ across F1/F2/F3' × low/mid/high modes (tight). **SE-S67-004-1 (Verifier-β substantive new content):** m≠0 IBP extension is formally derived with augmented bound (additional $2\max|h/k| + \int|(h/k)'|dr$ term, $h = 2me^\phi$); at canonical Branch-M sub-barrier electron mode ($m = m_e$, $E_1 = 2\sqrt{2}/3$, $E/m \sim 1$, $e^\phi \sim 0.6$ at typical $\phi$), $h/k \sim 0.625$ — second boundary term **O(1)** — bound is **vacuous** at this regime.

**S68-001 closure update (2026-05-15):** **Canonical Branch-C cosmological cubic α verification at §1.4.2 N=2 regular-origin scaffold anchor scale DERIVED.** Six cells (3 modes per κ at κ = ±1) × 3 fit windows = 18 cells with obs/bound $\in [0.38, 0.75]$ non-vacuous; cross-paradigm validated at Verifier-β scipy DOP853 x-coord to 4 sig figs. - **Within-single-observable sub-scope-partition at correlation-function-class observables (manuscript-grade observation, S75-001, 2026-05-18 post-S75-001 audit-first reconnaissance).** The "BAO galaxy auto-correlation" observable bifurcates structurally at canonical content into **AMPLITUDE sub-scope** (directional modulation of correlation function magnitude under canonical-UDT first-order-linear $\delta\phi_1$) and **SCALE sub-scope** (BAO peak characteristic length scale). CG §27 operator substrate transfers cleanly to AMPLITUDE sub-scope via pair-counts factor-of-2 modification (candidate closed-form $F^{(BAO\text{-}amp)} = 2(2 + x(1+\alpha))/3 = 2 F^{(NC)}$); SCALE sub-scope is canonical-content extension territory distinct from CG §27 operator transferability.
  - **Standard-ruler-not-available-at-canonical-UDT framing (load-bearing distinction).** LCDM cosmology uses the BAO peak as a **standard ruler** — the comoving sound horizon at recombination $r_d \approx 150$ Mpc treated as a fixed reference length whose apparent angular size at different redshifts measures expansion history. Canonical UDT is **STATIC** per Theory Rule 5; no recombination epoch in the LCDM expanding-universe sense; the BAO peak does NOT serve as a standard ruler at canonical UDT. What canonical UDT predicts is **amplitude modulation of the correlation function across the sky under directional $\delta\phi_1$**, NOT distance measurement via a fixed comoving reference scale. Sibling to LCDM-kinematic-vs-UDT-geometric standing prohibition #6 at observable-class scope — the structural distinction propagates from dipole-kinematic-vs-geometric distinction (number-count dipole) to standard-ruler-vs-amplitude-modulation distinction (BAO observable). Forward-pointer: any future BAO-class observable interpretation at canonical UDT must engage this distinction explicitly; the LCDM "standard ruler" framing is not transferable.
  - **Three modifications enumerated at S75-001 verdict.** M1: observable scope-narrowing to AMPLITUDE sub-scope at canonical-content first-order linear; "BAO observable" general sense is multi-modal and CG §27 addresses amplitude only. M2: pair-counts factor of 2 at first-order linear in small-pair-separation regime ($|\Delta r| \sim 150$ Mpc $\ll r_{\rm CMB} \sim 9$ Gpc; ratio ~1.7%; error $O(3\times 10^{-4})$). M3: BAO peak characteristic scale registered as separate canonical-content extension territory distinct from CG §27 operator transferability; distinct Charles tier-gate per S67-001 §V SE-S67-001-2 β + S70-001.
  - **Sibling-precedent registry advances 10 → 11-pattern** at TRANSFERS-WITH-MODIFICATIONS-AT-SUB-SCOPE class (S65-003 + S66-003 + S67-001 + S71-001b + S72-001 + S74-001-RETRY + S74-002 + **S75-001 within-single-observable sub-scope-bifurcation**). S75-001's bifurcation is into SUB-SCOPE-of-the-same-observable structural features (amplitude vs scale), not BIFURCATION-OF-FRAMINGS like S72-001 (aspherical-cavity Framing A vs matter-heterogeneity Framing B).
  - **Sibling-precedent class with S70-004a observable-class partition** (dipole-class vs amplitude-class at single-point observables; cross-observable class-partition scope) — S75-001 advances at sharper sub-scope (within-single-observable sub-scope-partition at correlation-function-class). - **Framework-neutral-vs-ΛCDM-processed observable classification as reusable methodology pattern (manuscript-grade observation, S75-003 Vε scope at S75-004 record-edit landing, 2026-05-18).** When comparing canonical-UDT predictions against published observational data, published values partition structurally into three classes that determine appropriateness for direct canonical-UDT comparison:
  - **Class (a) — Framework-neutral observables:** raw angular separations $\Delta\theta$ on sky; raw redshift separations $\Delta z$ along line-of-sight; raw flux correlations at high-$z$ (Lyman-α BAO closer than galaxy-correlation BAO to this scope); directional correlation amplitudes IF random-catalog construction methodology is framework-neutral. Appropriate for direct canonical-UDT-prediction comparison.
  - **Class (b) — ΛCDM-processed values:** $D_V(z) = [z \cdot D_M^2 \cdot D_H]^{1/3}$ volume-averaged distance (assumes FLRW $D_H/D_M \sim 1$-$3$ ratios that don't hold at canonical UDT where $D_H/D_M \sim 2$-$11\times$); $r_d$ sound horizon at drag epoch (rooted in baryon-photon plasma physics absent at canonical UDT; ΛCDM value $\sim 147.78$ Mpc vs canonical UDT $\sim 92$ Mpc geometric coherence scale per archived VR §34.6); $f\sigma_8(z)$ growth-rate combinations; fitted ΛCDM cosmological parameters. **Excluded from operative comparison** without explicit framework-translation discipline at observable-comparison layer.
  - **Class (c) — Boundary cases:** $D_M/r_d$ and $D_H/r_d$ ratios (numerator framework-neutral, denominator framework-loaded unless canonical-UDT-side-of-ratio uses canonical UDT $r_d$); hemispherical asymmetry analyses (framework-neutral at angular-test layer but may invoke ΛCDM template for amplitude normalization). Requires explicit canonical-UDT-side pinning before comparison.
  - **Reusable methodology scope:** applies to any canonical-UDT-vs-published-observable comparison — BAO observables (S75-001 → S75-002 → S75-003 arc), weak lensing two-point statistics, galaxy-cluster correlations, future BAO surveys, CMB-derived observables, SNe-class observables.

- **★ Kaleidoscope-class observational-channel quantity-identification recognition at canonical UDT — Vε SE-ε-4 NEW manuscript-grade observation (S77-002 verifier-surfaced, 2026-05-19).** Archived VR §34.6 UDT $r_d \sim 92$ Mpc is a **microphysical-cavity-channel projection** ($r_d = \pi r_*^{\rm CMB}/\ell_A^{\rm micro}$ per archived VR lines 213-215 verbatim); BAO-survey operational $r_d = \theta_{\rm BAO} \cdot D_M$ is the **angular galaxy-correlation feature scale** at framework-neutral observable scope. **These are kaleidoscope-class observational channel-distinct quantities at canonical UDT, both named "$r_d$"** — quantity-identification distinct, not algebraically equivalent.
